Provincial Order

Farmers May Use Grain as Collateral for Loans 140

The Shanghai County Government has received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, stating in essence: "Low grain prices harm farmers, a problem that has been lamented throughout history. This year's grain prices are particularly low, an unprecedented situation. If measures are not taken to provide relief, rural bankruptcy will occur, affecting the people's livelihood and having significant consequences. Various cooperatives should engage in the storage of essential food grains so that farmers can use grain as collateral for loans. Rural finance should rely on regulation. We are issuing regulations and ordering the county magistrate to comply accordingly." County Magistrate Pan ordered all county cooperatives yesterday to comply and report on their implementation for inspection.

Huasha Cotton Mill Seeds Picking

Cotton Merchants Request Temporary Suspension 141

Suggest Waiting for New Cotton to Market

Both Parties to Rectify in Production Areas

The Chinese Cotton Mill Association stated that recently, various mills have purchased cotton that contains a large amount of seed cotton or cotton seeds. Therefore, it has notified all mills to pick out cotton seeds and deduct them proportionally to avoid losses. It is now known that the local Cotton Ginning Industry Association and other trade associations have stated that this measure has caused great suffering to those engaged in the cotton business. They specially requested the mills to wait until the new cotton comes to market and for the mills and cotton merchants to jointly sort the cotton when purchasing goods in the production areas. Details are listed below.

Mill Announcement 142

The Chinese Cotton Mill Association previously issued an announcement stating: "According to reports from various mills, the cotton purchased recently contains a large amount of seed cotton or cotton seeds, resulting in significant invisible losses. The meeting has decided that in the future, if any cotton purchased by the mills is found to contain mixed seed cotton or cotton seeds, two bales out of every hundred bales will be taken out, and the cotton seeds or seed cotton that is picked out will be deducted proportionally according to the weight. This announcement is hereby issued to all members for compliance."

Cotton Merchants Expressed 143

The local Cotton Ginning Industry, Cotton Firm, Cotton Yarn Firm, Cotton Trading Firm, Cotton Distribution Merchants Association, and other trade associations have expressed their opinions to the Chinese Cotton Mill Association regarding the announcement of seed picking. In essence, they stated: "On February 18th of this year, your association announced that all members should comply with the seed picking notice. Upon hearing the news, the industry was alarmed. The Cotton Ginning Industry, Cotton Yarn Firm, Cotton Transportation Industry, and Cotton Trading Firm associations jointly convened a meeting to discuss the matter. The consensus was that improving cotton production should be supported, but since cotton from various regions has already been transported to the market, sudden picking and deduction will inevitably cause unexpected losses to those in transit. It was decided to send a letter requesting the mills to wait until the new cotton comes to market and for the mills and cotton merchants to jointly sort the cotton when purchasing goods in the production areas in order to implement the measure and achieve full effectiveness. After sending the letter, people were sent to consult, but there was no clear response. The mills, citing newspaper reports, have been strictly picking and deducting cotton, with no standards and inconsistencies, causing undue suffering to those engaged in the cotton business, without any restrictions. Investigating the rectification of cotton production and strictly prohibiting adulteration, our association presented a proposal to the Ministry of Industry in October 1931, which was approved and ordered to be circulated in cotton-producing areas. However, adulteration occurs in the production areas, not in the market. It is feared that not cracking down in the production areas but implementing the measures in the market is not a well-considered plan. Our association's request for a temporary suspension and joint rectification is nothing more than a fundamental plan to rectify cotton production. It is only a slight delay, and during the rectification process, it can avoid infringing on the interests of those in transit and promote smooth implementation. Otherwise, those who adulterate will suffer no loss, while cotton merchants will be exceptionally exploited. What could be more unfair than this? We are now reiterating our previous request, hoping that your association will publish a statement in the newspaper to temporarily suspend implementation. It is believed that your association's members and our association's colleagues have the friendship of hosts and guests and are as interdependent as lips and teeth, and will be able to consider both aspects and be happy to support this."

International Trade Association Council 144

Amending the Constitution and Reducing Membership Fees

The second council of the China International Trade Association held its first meeting at the Bank Club the other day. Those present were Pei Songsun, Xu Jiliu, Guo Bingwen, Pan Xulun, Zou Bingwen, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Xu Xinliu, etc. Zhang Gongquan was elected as chairman of the board, and Chen Guangfu, Guo Bingwen, Zou Bingwen, and Lin Kanghou were elected as executive directors. Pan Guangjiong was appointed as general secretary. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Shi Liangcai, the new director, resigned, and everyone unanimously asked him to stay. (2) The work plan was approved and submitted to the executive directors for research and implementation methods. (3) Tu Houbin suggested unified transportation and direct export, which was submitted to the executive directors for research. (4) The Overseas Chinese Trust Public Affairs Board of Directors suggested eight amendments to the Sino-British Commercial Treaty, which should be distributed to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Industry, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for verification and handling. (5) Amend the constitution and reduce membership fees. The annual fee for basic members, organizations, was reduced from 100 yuan to 50 yuan, the annual fee for individuals was reduced from 30 yuan to 20 yuan, and the annual fee for ordinary members was reduced from 10 yuan to 5 yuan. It is also planned to broadly solicit various industry colleagues and professional scholars to join.

Light Tax Diesel

Investigation of Applicability to Engines 145

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce stated that the Ministry of Finance's increase in the import tax rate on diesel has had a significant impact on various industries that use diesel as fuel for machinery. It has requested the Ministry of Finance to postpone the implementation of the new tax standards in order to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. Subsequently, the Ministry of Finance replied that the diesel tax rate was originally divided into two types, A and B, and has not been increased uniformly. Among the light-tax diesel fuels, there are also those that can be applied to engines and other machinery. Therefore, the newly established diesel tax standards do not hinder various industries that use diesel as fuel for machinery. According to a reporter's investigation, the Special Solar Oil sold on the market is the light-tax diesel listed in the Ministry of Finance's new tax regulations. Experts from factories in various regions believe that it is suitable for diesel engine fuel. For example, the National diesel engine from Jardine Matheson, the Gardner diesel engine from William Jacks & Co., the Ruston diesel engine from Andersen, Meyer & Co., the Deutz diesel engine from Jebsen & Co., and the Blackstone diesel engine from Dodwell & Co. are all very suitable. Currently, the Hengyuanxiang Cotton Ginning Factory in Pudong, Shanghai, the Chengyu Cotton Ginning Factory, the Shengtailou Steamboat Company, the Shaoxing Daming Electric Light Company, the Nanjing Datong Flour Mill, the Pinghu Pinghu Electric Light Company, and others have all used this special solar oil to reduce fuel costs.

Shanghai County

Land Survey and Preparation of General Map 146

The basic work of setting up the control points for the land survey in Shanghai County has been completed. Currently, the Department of Land Administration of the Province is assigning a survey team to measure the traverse lines, and the household land survey will be conducted soon. However, the county government believes that the location names recorded in the land deeds for private land transactions in the county and the township and district map preservation numbers used by the collection office to calculate the area and tax amount are still used for convenience. It has now been decided that this survey will use the original maps as units, but the boundaries must be reorganized. According to the existing 74 maps, numbers will be assigned from No. 1 to No. 74. Lands that were previously surveyed with interspersed plots will be included in the calculation of the land in this map, and under the newly compiled map name in the current map book, the original map number will be noted for reference. Now, in order to understand the original township and district boundaries of each district for easy reference during the survey, the county government has specially prepared rough maps of each district and the names of the township and district maps, and has ordered the district chiefs to comply, immediately investigate and clarify the boundaries of all township and district maps within their jurisdiction, as well as the names of the villages where the boundaries are located, and mark and test the boundaries in the issued rough map of the district and submit them to the county for compiling a general map and forwarding it to the survey team for application.

Russian Lai Weiciji is a well-known international fraudster. He was once arrested by the Public Concession Police and handed over to the First Special District Court for sentencing and punishment. First, Lai, posing as French Vice-Consul Bai Leai, ordered his accomplice Luo Mainuofu to pose as the French police chief inspector to lead Xu to the French Consulate in December of last year, pretending to introduce him to Lai (i.e., the alias Bai Leai). Lai falsely claimed to be the French Vice-Consul and said that the chief inspector (referring to Luo Mainuofu) was a close friend who could help him obtain a club license (i.e., a gambling den), but a large amount of lobbying fees would be required to succeed. Xu and others believed it to be true and immediately ordered Fan to register in his name. On the afternoon of the 28th (the other day), at about 7 p.m., they hosted a banquet at the D. Doutremeline Restaurant on Sichuan Road to discuss the organization of a large-scale gambling den with the fake chief inspector and fake vice-consul. After Xu met with these people, he immediately ordered Zhou to rent a large Western-style empty house at No. 634 Lane, Xiafei Road, actively renovating it, waiting for the license to be issued before opening. However, the matter was detected by Chief Inspector Jin Jiulin of the Support Police, who ordered Secretary Qian Renlong to disguise himself as a dinner guest and participate in their banquet. During the banquet, Lai demanded 30,000 yuan as lobbying fees for the consulate and the police. Just as they were discussing the matter, Secretary Qian used the telephone to report to Chief Inspector Jin and Deputy Chief Inspector Warren, Inspector Greilishi, Russian Detective Faraofu, and Chinese and Western detectives. Together with the Public Police, they arrested the entire group of perpetrators and brought them to the police station, waiting to be handed over to the Second Court for interrogation.

Dies Tragically Under Wheels 149

Xiangsheng Chauffeur Causes Trouble

Police Still Need to Investigate

On the afternoon of the 27th, the Xiangsheng Automobile Company sent chauffeur Zhang Zhiyun, a local, to drive car No. 18462 on a business trip to Tongfu Road. At about 5 p.m., Zhang was driving south to north on Route Mayerciere in the French Concession, when Liu Bangfu, a 73-year-old man from Tongzhou who lived nearby, went out to buy tin foil and was walking on the side of the road. The driver, Zhang, was careless and the car rushed out of the street edge, knocking Liu down and injuring his head. Patrolman No. 556 found the accident and sent Liu to Guangci Hospital while taking Zhang and the car to the police station for investigation. Liu, due to his old age and severe injuries, died shortly after being admitted to the hospital. The hospital notified the police station, and the Vehicle Affairs Office sent a detective to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for autopsy. The next day, the Second Special District Court was asked to send someone to investigate and clarify the matter. The body was collected by Liu Yukun, a member of the family. In the afternoon, the Vehicle Affairs Office sent the defendant Zhang Zhiyun to the First Criminal Tribunal of the Second Special Court. Judge Wang Gangxu conducted a preliminary hearing. Police lawyer Fei Xizhen explained the case, stating that the Vehicle Affairs Office's investigation was not yet complete and requested a postponement until the case was clarified before proceeding with the trial. The defendant was defended by lawyer Shen Xiaoxiang. The court briefly questioned the defendant about the circumstances of the accident and then ordered that the hearing be postponed until the investigation was completed. The defendant was temporarily detained at the police station.

From Fingerprints

A Recidivist Abductor Is Identified 158

Zhang Jinshan Entices Lu Aqing

Lu Aqing, a child from Jiangyin, ten years old, came to Shanghai to learn to be a coppersmith. He was reprimanded by his master and went out. He met abductor Zhang Jinshan (31 years old, from Ningbo), who enticed him to visit the City God Temple in the city. Because Lu wanted to go home, the abductor wanted to trick him to the pier. Lu was afraid that his master would chase him, and he looked flustered. Li Mingjun of the 22nd post saw him and found him suspicious, so he questioned him. Lu was dazed. Then someone nearby asked the child in the Jiangyin dialect, and he said that he did not know the man and that he had taken him to visit the City God Temple, etc. It was clearly an abduction. He was immediately taken to the police station for investigation. After questioning Lu, Director Liu learned that the defendant's name was Zhang Jinshan. When asked about his occupation and address, he was vague. When asked about his relationship with Lu, he gave evasive answers. Then Director Liu checked the fingerprint book and found that the defendant had been punished for abducting children before. He was undoubtedly an abductor and was sentenced to be sent to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegram to the Guizhou Provincial Government

Exemption from Import Tax on Chinese-Made Electric Fans 161

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Guangxi Provincial Government, stating, "On the 27th of this month, we received a letter from the Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industry Association, stating that the member association, Huasheng Electric Factory, has stated in a letter that the various electric fans manufactured by our factory are imported into Guangxi every year in considerable quantities. When these fans are exported, tax silver is paid to the Shanghai Customs. Recently, it has been heard that the Guangxi Provincial Government levies a tax on these fans when they enter the province. If this is true, we are deeply concerned that the cost will increase, making it impossible to compete with foreign goods. Our factory is the first factory in China to manufacture electrical appliances, and it has been fighting against foreign goods for many years, which is well known to society. If the tax in Guizhou Province is increased, it will be difficult to sell, which will have a great impact on the national products industry. Therefore, we hereby request that your association forward our request to Chairman Huang of the Guangxi Provincial Government, asking him to consider the budding national products and order his subordinates to exempt our factory's electric fans from the tax on entering the province, in order to show maintenance and benefit the sales of national products, which is a public consensus. In the past, when the Likin tax in our country was not abolished, all foreign-style goods imitated by Chinese merchants using machinery, in addition to paying export tax at the port of shipment, were not taxed again, no matter which province they were transported to for sale, so as to encourage domestic products and compete with foreign goods. Now that the Likin tax has been abolished, there is no possibility of re-taxation, and the method of paying only one tax on foreign goods imitated by machinery has been in effect until now and has not changed. Your province has always been known for encouraging the development of industries and benefiting businesses. The Huasheng Electric Machinery Factory's electric fans, which are made by Chinese people, should be protected according to law when they are transported and sold in your province. It is appropriate to allow them to be exempted from import tax, which is a public convenience. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce bows respectfully."

The Sinking of the Sanjiang Steamer

It Can Be Towed Back to Shanghai Soon When the Water Rises 163

The Ningjing Steamer of the Ningjing-Ningshao Company ran aground on the Huifeng Reef upstream of Anqing in November last year while sailing from Hankou to Shanghai. The hull was damaged, and the bottom was stranded high on the reef. The river water was shallow and there was no way to escape. Therefore, the damaged parts were repaired first, and the crew and stewards were temporarily dismissed, waiting for the spring high water period this year to find a way to tow it back to Shanghai. It has been more than five months since then. The losses suffered by the steamer this time, including the company's loss of schedule business, is about 60,000 yuan. The dismissal of crew members and various expenses during the grounding period is about 30,000 yuan. The losses in hull insurance and repair costs also require 50,000 to 60,000 yuan, totaling 140,000 to 150,000 yuan. Now that the Yangtze River is rising, it is expected to be towed back to Shanghai for repairs within two weeks.

Emei: The Emei Steamer of the China Merchants Bureau ran aground on the Huatanzi Reef in the Sichuan River in June last year. The hull was stranded on a reef more than 20 feet high. The bureau sent the chief captain to tow it. After several months, the cost reached more than 100,000 yuan. Finally, the reef at the bottom of the ship was blasted away with explosives, and the hull was able to rest on the bank of the river. Now we have received a telegram from the captain, Ji Qingrong, stating that the Sichuan River is about to rise, and the Emei Steamer can soon float out of the shoal on its own during the high water. At that time, it can be towed into the heart of the river and return to Shanghai immediately. Preparations for towing assistance are now underway.

Qingpu: The Qingpu Steamer of the Sanbei Company ran aground on the levee at the Digang Wharf. The chief captain personally went to find a way to move the hull flat, causing it to be stranded for several months, but the hull was not broken. The company's direct and indirect losses amounted to more than 100,000 yuan. Now that the river water is rising day by day, the steamer also has hope of emerging from the shoal and can return to Shanghai for repairs in three weeks at the latest. In addition, the Taikoo Anqing Steamer, which ran aground in the fields on the bank of the Yangtze River at Qingshanzui, has now been sold by the company. First, the machinery was removed, and then the hull was dismantled, and Taikoo has given up operating the steamer on the Yangtze River.

Shishan Lane's Water Bill Dispute

Tenants Convened an Emergency Meeting Yesterday 168

The tenants of Shishan Lane, Huade Road, in this city have repeatedly received notices from the British-owned Shanghai Water Company, urging each household to pay a deposit of nine yuan for the installation of water meters, otherwise the water will be cut off. However, all the tenants in the lane believe that the water meter and water bill have always been borne by the owner, so it is not convenient to take direct action. Moreover, the installation of sub-water meters has not been agreed to by all the tenants. The company has installed them without authorization, so they have ignored them. Yesterday, the water company again notified the tenants of the lane to quickly sign the meter installation contract with the company and pay the deposit, otherwise the water will be cut off by the end of this month. The tenants of the lane immediately appointed Zhou Fuzhang as a representative to complain to the owner about the suffering of not being able to bear the burden, and in order to be done once and for all, contributed the idea of digging an artesian well in the lane to avoid the danger of water cuts. The property manager received them and agreed to forward them to the owner for consideration and then reply. However, the owner did not understand the suffering of the tenants and extended the lease to Fenling Lawyers to send a letter to the representative Zhou Zhuanzhang, warning him and making excuses for rent arrears, and preventing all the tenants from paying the deposit, and ordering them to leave the house within a month. This caused the anger of the tenants, who convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon and resolved that if the owner oppressed Zhou Jun, they were willing to swear to protect him to the end, regardless of any sacrifice.

Anhui Series

The Third Phase Will Be Published 170

The Anhui Series Compilation and Printing Office has published two phases of books, totaling 34 types, mostly taken from the most valuable works of the Anhui sages, reproduced in photo-offset from the original fine editions. In the first phase of books, such as Huang Yuesong's "Yu Gong Jin Shi" from Dangtu, Wang Long's "Mao Shi Yi Yi" from Shexian, Zhou Tingcai's "Han Shi Wai Zhuan Xiao Zhu" from Jixi, Wu Lang's "Wu Sheng Fan Qie Zheng Jun" from Quanjiao, Zhao Shaozu's "Tong Jian Zhu Shang" from Jingxian, Zhao Jixu's "Han Ru Zhuan Jing Ji" from Xiuning, Cheng Tong's "Xin'an Xue Xi," Abbot Jianjiang's Painting Gatha, and Jiang Yunning's Collection of Poems, are all books that scholars must read. The second phase of books is Cheng Yaotian's "Tong Yi Lu" from Shexian, with the addition of unpublished manuscripts and four kinds of lost works, which can be called perfect compared with the old edition. The original edition of "Tong Yi Lu" was priced at hundreds of tens of gold. Now, the increased printing price is only ten yuan, so as soon as the book came out, buyers rushed to buy it. It is indeed a great opportunity for scholars. It is said that the third phase of the series has been sent to press and will be published in about two months. It is said that the book list in this phase includes Yu Zhengxie's "Guiyi Lei Gao," which was personally revised in his later years, Jiang Yong's "Yun Xue San Shu," and Huang Sheng's "Zi Gu Yi Fu He An," among others. Yu's manuscript has been revised by nearly one-third of the original edition and has not been circulated. It is now borrowed from a book collector in Yixian by the office and sent to press in accordance with Yu's manuscript to preserve the true traces. Jiang's Yun Shu was finely proofread and carved in Jinling by Lu Lifu, the governor of Liangjiang during the Xianfeng period, who invited the phonology experts Xia Yu and Xia Xie from Dangtu. The entire plate was destroyed when the Taiping Army went east. Only ten copies were printed at that time, and they became rare treasures. "Zi Gu Yi Fu He An" is also a rare book on the market. The above-mentioned types are indeed special books for studying history, phonology, philology, and textual research, and are books that scholars must have. It is also said that the fourth and fifth phase book lists have also been finalized and will be issued for the world this year.

First Voice of the Die Lai Hotel in West Lake 172

West Lake in Hangzhou is the most beautiful scenic spot in our country. It is surrounded by green mountains in the west, south, north, and the sparkling waves and misty shadows complement each other. In spring, warblers greet people, and in autumn, the bright moon clears the waves. In hot summer, the lotus breeze sends the evening coolness, and in the cold winter, the plum blossoms condense the snow. Ancient temples and villas, famous scenic spots and historical sites, are especially solemn and beautiful, making people happy and reluctant to leave, comparable to the famous Geneva in the world. Chen Xiaodie, a businessman and artist in this city, believes that such a famous scenic spot lacks a magnificent, well-equipped, quiet environment and attentive service, so he feels that it is a fly in the ointment. He has specially founded and organized a Die Lai Hotel next to Xiling Bridge to meet the needs of Chinese and foreign travelers. Its location is suitable and elegant, the equipment is perfect and clean, the waiters are attentive, and the architecture is exquisite and comfortable. It is a new highlight for the hotel industry and a record for the construction industry. He has now gathered comrades and is actively proceeding.

Tenants of Fu Run Li Request a Delay in Demolition 176

The An He Company, landlord of Fu Run Li and De Run Li in Nanshi's Nine Mu Di area, issued a notice on the 23rd of this month, requiring all tenants to vacate by May 16th to facilitate reconstruction. The total number of tenant households in the area is over one thousand, with a population of over ten thousand. Since receiving this notice, the community has been in a state of panic, as the buildings in the area are not old and their interiors are still exceptionally sturdy. Moreover, at a time of economic recession and hardship for the people, they cannot afford the cost of relocation. Therefore, they have collectively opposed the demolition and are taking unified action, requesting a delay in reconstruction. They have already initiated the organization of a mutual aid association and convened a meeting yesterday afternoon, attended by over two hundred tenant representatives. Reported matters: (1) A letter has been sent to the landlord requesting a five-year delay in reconstruction. (2) All necessary procedures have been properly handled. (3) The association has appointed fifteen committee members. Matters for discussion: (1) Those tenants in the area who voluntarily join have already signed up, but further review is required. Resolved: Approved. (2) How should the association raise temporary funds? Resolved: Temporarily funded voluntarily by the committee members, without collecting from each household. (3) Tenants should be notified not to cause any damage before the case is resolved. Resolved: Approved. (4) How should rental issues be handled? Resolved: Tenants should pay their rent as usual. If the accounting office comes to collect, tenants should not refuse to pay, and tenants must continue to pay monthly as before. Other active measures, such as posting slogans, issuing declarations, and requesting assistance, are being taken. It is said that the tenants in the area are maintaining a peaceful attitude but are demonstrating extreme unity.

Although the writing was incomprehensible, it was clear that he had taken poison and attempted suicide, and he seemed to be suffering from poisoning. A police chief was sent to take him to the Red Cross for rescue. However, the reason for the suicide is unknown. After he recovers, he will be reported to the District General Bureau for investigation and assistance.

Letter Received 186

To the esteemed editor of Shenbao:

I am writing to you regarding the news item in the "Local News" column of your newspaper on the 29th, "Ronglin Warehouse Resumes Work Under Police Protection by the Public Security Bureau," which states that the details mentioned are not factual. I am writing to request a correction as follows:

Our warehouse was rented to Yuchang Coal Company for storage in 1927 and renamed Ronglin Warehouse Yuji, with a contract stipulating that it would be returned at the end of July 1933 due to unpaid rent. We had Mr. Tao Jiachun, a lawyer, publish an announcement to clarify the situation. When Yuchang Coal Company rented the warehouse, Li Xiahong contracted to load and unload coal. Now that Ronglin Warehouse is operating on its own, it is reasonable to recruit our own loaders. We immediately advertised for bids, and the workers' representative, Qiu Antai, won the contract. This led to the obstruction of work by Li Xiahong, the foreman of Yuchang Coal Company, who almost resorted to violence. Fortunately, the Municipal Party Committee, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and the Public Security Bureau sent personnel to mediate and decided to abolish any foreman system. Unexpectedly, shortly after the start of work, Li Xiahong came out to obstruct again, and a strike ensued. We immediately applied to handle the conclusion of all outstanding matters, entrusted to Yitaixing Nan Warehouse as an agent. However, Xie Peide, the manager of Yitaixing Nan Warehouse, still contracted with Li Xiahong under the foreman system, violating the Bureau of Social Affairs' instruction to abolish the foreman system. Our warehouse believes that this is related to the credibility of the Municipal Party Committee, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and the Public Security Bureau and is unwilling to recognize it. This time, all the workers requested to resume work due to livelihood issues. The Party and government agencies have repeatedly summoned both parties to mediate wages, but the foreman has repeatedly failed to appear. The Party and government agencies believe that the evil influence of a foreman cannot be allowed to hinder the work of the warehouse and endanger the lives of all workers. Therefore, the warehouse was approved to hire another foreman to continue work, and two teams of police officers were dispatched to the site to monitor and protect it, and unloading has resumed as usual. However, fearing that the reports are inaccurate, we are making this correction. I wish you well,

Ronglin Warehouse, Pudong

March 29th

Letter Received

Fundraising Appeal for the Kalachakra Initiation Ceremony 187

In the past, when the Panchen Lama came north, he was invited to Hangzhou to preach the Dharma, but it did not come to fruition due to unripe conditions. In the summer of 1931, people in Peiping and Tianjin advocated for the construction of the Kalachakra assembly, and after years of preparation, it was held in the Hall of Supreme Harmony in the autumn of the following year. After seven days of completion, more than 100,000 people were initiated and received the Dharma, which was an unprecedented grand event in China. Benefactors in the southeast, due to the distance and obstacles, had few participants and their wishes were not fulfilled. Now that the master has come to Beijing, his colleagues have renewed their previous request and received a merciful approval, which is scheduled to be held at the Lingyin Ancient Temple in West Lake, starting on April 28 this year (March 15 of the lunar calendar), to initiate the Kalachakra Initiation Ceremony. Here, we will briefly explain its meaning to our ten-way good people. As the saying goes, blessings are born from a foundation, and misfortunes are born from a womb. Planting causes yields results, without the slightest deviation. This has been the case since ancient times, and it is even more so today. In recent years, our country has been plagued by natural disasters and man-made disasters, internal and external troubles, coming one after another. The suffering of the people exceeds that of the late Tang and Five Dynasties. Moreover, the powers are competing to expand their military preparations, weapons of destruction are being innovated every day, conventions are being broken, the economy is declining, and a world war is imminent. The future misery will be greater and wider than hundreds of times before. It can be said with certainty that the coming of this great disaster is due to the ripening of karmic retribution, and the reason for its invitation is due to the common cause. To try to save it, we must unite the masses of people to communicate with it. Therefore, in ancient times, when a disaster occurred, the superiors blamed themselves, and the subordinates cultivated and reflected, which was enough to inspire the harmony of heaven and eliminate the misfortune without shape. Today, the human heart is decaying, and without the blessing of the Buddha's power, there is no way to eliminate this vast catastrophe. The Kalachakra Sutra is the head of the five great vajras of the unsurpassed esoteric vehicle. It discusses the sun, moon, stars, and rocks on top, and the essence, qi, and meridians of the human body below. Those who master this sutra can verify the solar eclipse, the lunar eclipse, and the delay in the wind and rain by their own bodies, and they are all accurate. Its vastness and subtlety are truly inconceivable. Moreover, the six realms of sentient beings, when encountering this supreme cause, can obtain initiation even if they do not come to the altar to contemplate and visualize, or they can deeply plant the roots of the Buddha if they have not sought the Dharma in accordance with the rituals, but have only heard the sound of the bell, seen the altar rituals, or even heard the name of the Kalachakra Vajra. If those who have participated in this assembly and can sincerely visualize, and are covered by the guru's dedication, they will receive the benefits of the Dharma, regardless of distance. This is not only to eliminate disasters. According to the records of the great virtues of the Western Regions, the First Panchen Lama was once the head of the Shambhala, and he will be reborn in that land in the future. Now, inviting his incarnation to respond to the situation should have special merits and virtues. In the past, the Yuan, Ming, and Qing Dynasties supported the Lamas and presided over national affairs, which were established as examples. The Panchen Lama is the teacher of our country. In this time of frequent turmoil and universal terror, we should sincerely invite him to borrow the power of the Dharma to eliminate disasters for the country and pray for peace for the world. However, this matter is of great importance and requires a great amount of money, which cannot be accomplished by a small number of people. It should be requested that benefactors from all directions, regardless of country or race, contribute according to their ability and practice generosity, so that we can accumulate soil into mountains, and small streams return to the sea. We will plant the same good causes, eliminate common karma, turn disaster into good fortune, all in this move.

Kalachakra Initiation Ceremony Office Regulations Article 1: This office is fully responsible for the preparation of all matters related to the Kalachakra Initiation Ceremony until it is completed. Article 2: This office shall have a number of directors, who shall be publicly elected by the initiators, one chairman, six vice-chairmen, and a number of executive directors, who shall be mutually elected by the board of directors. Article 3: The chairman represents this office externally and is responsible for all matters internally. The vice-chairmen assist the chairman in the execution of all matters. The executive directors shall be present every day to plan the progress and handle all daily affairs. Article 4: The business of this office shall be divided into the following five groups: (1) General Affairs Group: Managing the distribution of affairs and matters not belonging to each group. (2) Dharma Affairs Group: Handling all matters related to the Dharma practice. (3) Document Group: Handling notices, letters, telegrams, and safekeeping of all documents. (4) Economic Group: Handling fundraising and financial matters. (5) Propagation Group: Handling the propagation of the Dharma assembly. Article 5: Each group shall have one director and two deputy directors, who shall be elected by the board of directors, and a number of staff members, who shall be appointed by the chairman, to manage the affairs of each group. Article 6: The meetings of this office shall be divided into the board of directors meeting, the full staff meeting, and the group meeting. The board of directors meeting and the full staff meeting shall be convened by the directors, and the group meeting shall be convened by the director. There is no fixed schedule. Article 7: All staff members of this office are honorary positions. Employees and servants may be given appropriate salaries. Article 8: These regulations shall take effect upon approval by the initiators' meeting.

Reading Q&A

How to Study the Constitution 188

(1) Question

Reading Guidance

Recently, the government's Legislative Yuan released a draft constitution, hoping that everyone will offer opinions. I think we don't even understand what a constitution is, so how can we offer opinions? Sir, is it necessary for everyone to understand the constitution? What is the relationship between the constitution and the general public? What are the advantages and disadvantages of a good or bad constitution for the people? I hope to know all these things, but I don't know how to start studying it. Please give me an answer!

Lin Henwo, letter

(2) Answer

Mr. Lin's questions are indeed questions in the minds of the general public. Nowadays, most people are really too indifferent to politics. One of the reasons is that discussing state affairs often offends people, so according to the principle of "self-preservation," it is best to "not talk" about it. But this is not the biggest reason. The biggest reason is that in recent years, there have been too many political opinions, policies, political programs, etc. in opposition, and political facilities, etc. in power, and they all sound very nice and seem to have a lot of reasons. But until now, not only has the stable life that the general public needs not been achieved, but there is also the crisis of Japan's forcible seizure of Manchuria and Mongolia, France's occupation of the Nine Small Islands, and Britain's coveting of "Panhong," etc. There is also the personal pain of poverty, unemployment, hunger, and cold. As a result, the general public has become desperate and no longer wants to pay attention to all political propositions and facilities. This is right, but it is also wrong. The reason why it is right is that these propositions are an unfulfilled check, completely a set of manipulative tricks. But our politics, although bad, are not without hope of clarity, and our lives, although extremely painful, are not without a future of welfare. Therefore, it is a very serious mistake for us to be discouraged by politics and lose interest. It must be known that the more we do not study politics, the more opportunities there will be for all kinds of deceptive tricks, and the more practical theories that expose the truth will be despised, leading to a lack of clarity between right and wrong, and a confusion of black and white, and the worse the politics, the more painful our lives will be. Therefore, our attitude towards politics should not only be passive indifference, but also active research. Only in this way can we avoid being deceived by propaganda that distorts the facts, and only in this way can we recognize our future. We will never be pessimistic or depressed, but will have the determination to fight and work hard. Judging from Mr. Lin's letter, it seems that he still has a bit of an "indifferent" attitude towards studying politics, so I am taking this opportunity to discuss it.

What is a constitution? Let's not define it now, but first say what the content of the constitution is, what it includes, because knowing what the content of the constitution is, we will also know what the constitution is. The content of the constitution includes two kinds, one is substantive, and the other is formal. The formal content is to discuss the status of the constitution, the procedures for its enactment and amendment, and where it differs from ordinary laws. The substantive content is to talk about what the constitution is supposed to stipulate. The formal content has little to do with the constitution that we want to know, so let's put it aside for now. Of course, this does not mean that it has no relationship with the constitution or is not important. The substantive content of the constitution can be divided into three types: First, it stipulates the people's right to participate in politics, discussing whether the people have the right to actually manage the country, and the scope of that right. Second, the form of state power, which is divided into two aspects. One is to say the source of political power, or to whom it belongs, such as a minority or majority dictatorship, etc., and the relationship between the executive and the legislative. The other is to say the division of powers between the central and local governments. Third, are the main goals that the country wants to achieve, or in simpler terms, what the country wants to do. This part includes many of the country's basic laws, etc.

That is roughly what a constitution is, now let's talk about the method of studying the constitution.

First, studying the constitution should not only look at the meaning on paper, but should also observe whether it can be realized, that is, whether its ideals or goals have the possibility of being realized in the society at that time. In other words, we must study the essence of the content of the constitution, and not be deceived by its rhetoric.

Ordinary capitalist countries boast of democratic politics. Whether it is a republic or a constitutional monarchy, the constitution stipulates that everyone has the right to participate in politics, everyone is equal under the law, and everyone has freedom of assembly, association, publication, and speech. But what is the reality? Still, the rich and powerful hold the political power, and the rulers are still a class of literati and officials. In so-called democratic or constitutional monarchy countries, elections are manipulated by a group of political parties, which flaunt various political programs and policies for the country and the people in order to win over voters and compete in elections. In fact, they are only loyally serving a minority of people, and the political programs and policies are just a facade. However, the elected representatives cannot do without them. Therefore, it is very easy for a minority of people in society to monopolize political power in order to oppress the majority. They can buy some political parties, or send people to organize some political parties and let them campaign and strive for political power. If these political parties are in power, then those few people, although they appear to be the same as ordinary people on the surface, without any special privileges, can actually influence the politics of a country. Therefore, the sovereignty of the people as a whole, as stipulated in the constitution, is a bowl of hypnotic soup, an attempt to cover up the mask of a minority monopolizing the political machine. (To be continued)

Reply to Xu Kejun, Xinjian, Pinghu: Please provide a detailed address for a reply.

Chunqiu

I Have a Few Words to Say (Continued) 189

— Lean Wren

We are originally very welcoming of anecdotes about famous people. But for some reason? Every time we publish a passage about the anecdotes of great men and gentlemen, it always has to be passively corrected the next day. The author thinks it is hearsay about morality and can be used as material; the editor thinks it can be used as a topic of conversation after tea and wine; both parties have no intention and no effect. However, based on my many years of editing experience, this kind of anecdote about great men and gentlemen is really debatable and un-debatable; publishable and un-publishable. Some readers may think it is sucking up or bootlicking, while the great men and gentlemen themselves think it is a joke, scolding the mountain gate. Therefore, from now on, we will no longer welcome anecdotes about contemporary celebrities, and it is better to be "careful of fire" ourselves than to cause trouble.

In the bottom row, don't we often have things like "Travels," "Women's Corner," "World Wonders," and "Small Recipes?" There are many such categories. In addition to the four types mentioned above, there are also ten types such as "Scientific Anecdotes," "Small Knowledge," "Short Stories," "Laughter Mobilization," "Miscellaneous Talks," "Local Chronicles," "Small Gardening," "Small Handicrafts," "One-Act Plays," and "Mini-Novels." All novel and meaningful materials are welcomed. However, the number of words in each type is limited to a maximum of 1,000 words, because if there are too many, they will be arranged in densely packed layers, like ants carrying dead flies, which is too ugly, and the old gentlemen whose eyesight has been discounted can only sigh at the "words."

Comics were originally published once a week in the bottom row, usually with four or five pictures together. Now we also plan to change it to one picture per day. For example, eating a table of assorted dishes every week, although it feels rich, is not as appetizing as eating the same delicacy every day. In addition to Huang Shiying, Zhang Yingchao, and Jiang Dongliang, who are responsible for this type of comics, submissions are also welcome. The title pictures are best in the form of patterns, and the size must be three-quarters larger than the current size set by this publication, so that it can be reduced for plate making.

Whether it is a manuscript or a painting, the author's name and address must be indicated, and a seal must be affixed. The number of words must be indicated on the manuscript. These three things are considered the three chapters of the law between this publication and the authors. If you are unwilling to comply, then after publication, remuneration will be discussed later, and I will not be polite. (Attached statement: Whether or not the submitted manuscripts are published, they will not be returned.) At the beginning of the transformation of "Spring and Autumn," the book "Memoirs of the Court of Peking," translated by Qin Shouou, is specially published as a memorial. This book was written in English by Princess Der Ling of the former Qing Dynasty, also known as "The Old Buddha's Era of the Empress Dowager Cixi," and records the secret history of the Qing Palace at that time, which is very interesting. Mr. Qin is originally a famous novelist, and his translation is also exquisite and pleasing, and he does not lose the original meaning at all. The purpose of our publishing this book is not to make readers feel any "ancient sentiment," but just like inviting everyone to watch Mei Lanfang perform a "Taizhen Biography" on stage.

"Spring and Autumn" is about to change. But from which day does it start to change? Well! April 1, 1934 (The Children's Weekly that should have been published on this day will be moved to Children's Day on April 4).

The Water in the Vase Should Be Drunk as Tea 190

— Dew

This title is very witty, and some people may regard it as a witty story. In fact, the author wrote it with tears in his eyes.

A few days ago, a certain lady sent a letter to the editor of the local supplement of this newspaper. She said, "......I am a vase in a certain office. Among several vases, that ×× actually took a fancy to me. ......He came to flirt with me twice last year, but I cleverly avoided them. ......Now he has gone a step further and opened a hotel room. ......I struggled all night, but I didn't succumb. ......If I resign from this position? I will have to watch my parents, brothers and sisters starve! ......So I think I can only take the path of Ms. Ai Xia. ......" After reading this record, we can know that women's occupation is really a serious problem today. For the lawlessness of a certain ××, not only is his personal character bankrupt, but he is also one of the major criminals who destroy women's occupation. However, let's not talk about him here for the time being.

In this era, it is too unlucky to be a woman. Especially those with beautiful looks are even more dangerous. So how unfortunate is the production of the word "vase", and how painful it is! However, the vase is ultimately something for people to appreciate, and there is a warning of "can be seen but not moved" in this meaning. At best, it can only be said that it is "impractical." I think Ms. So-and-so, it is better to comfort yourself well and not take the path of Ms. Ai Xia! Because what I have is two treasures, one is life and the other is the soul. As long as I don't sell my soul, the harm to my life, the blows to my mind, and the difficulties in life are nothing! If you sell your soul, then there is no place to say the bitterness!

Finally, I also hope that working women will broaden your horizons in the future, prepare your true knowledge, and study more professional skills. On the one hand, you should also be frugal and not raise your life above your level. In this way, you will no longer be a vase, and no one will drink the water in the vase as tea! Otherwise, even if you are not a vase, you will get other patterns!

Research on Inkstones (10) (3) 192

— Bored Guest

▲ Overview of Duan Inkstones

(3) Stone Flaws: The history of inkstones lists fifteen kinds of stone flaws. However, many of these fifteen kinds have gradually become beautiful patterns due to the shift in aesthetic psychology. Generally, it is because the flaws are hard and do not affect the ink in the ink pool, and the patterns are indeed worth seeing; or because the flaws do not change the nature of the stone at all and can increase the beauty; or because the flaws are unique to the lower cliff or the Da Xi Cave and can be used as proof of a good stone. Inkstone lovers observe this kind of stone from various aspects and only feel that it is valuable and not a disease. This is the reason why stone flaws become beautiful patterns. Try to record the stone flaws separately.

(A) Stone flaws that are called beautiful patterns

1. Emerald Pattern: Congealed green like sprinkled juice, also known as emerald dots, there are two kinds of heavy green and light green, with the same veins as the eye, only yellow-green is not enough weight, green is loved by everyone. 2. Yellow Dragon Pattern: Grayish yellow like a dragon and snake slanting on the stone is called Yellow Dragon. The color is burnt and astringent and contains earthy gas, and it is a stone disease if it is horizontal in the heart of the inkstone. If it is bright and reveals the light of golden sand, or is hidden in the shape of a small golden circle, it is very beautiful.

2. Jade Belt: White and solidified green that is slender and long, or pure white, is called Jade Belt. It is mellow, clean, and extremely beautiful. There is also a white stripe that is about twice the size of a gold and silver thread, called a white stripe pattern. A slight tinge of tender green is called a green stripe pattern, which are all kinds of jade belts.

3. Jade Dot: A white dot as large as a mung bean is called a jade dot, also known as a pomegranate kernel. It is very difficult to obtain if it is refined, crystal clear, tender, and moist. 5. Gold and Silver Thread: Occasionally one or two threads are seen on the inkstone surface. The veins are yellow, which is called a gold thread pattern, and the white is called a silver thread pattern. Scholars love those that are fine and do not damage the hairs, but those that are rough are not taken.

4. Sparrow Spots: Spots similar to ink scars are called sparrow spots, also known as partridge spots. The spots are purple-brown and quite spectacular. If the spots are slightly longer and form dense rows like sparrow spots, they are called pine bark patterns, which are medium and second-class products.

5. Five-Colored Nails: There are two kinds of five-colored nails, white and green. Although they are firm and resistant to blades, they are only found in the Da Xi Cave, and they are even more valuable because they are glittering with precious light. The history of inkstones also has so-called cinnabar nails, also known as cinnabar spots, which are bright and colorful, and are most valuable if they are not in the ink pool (Da Xi Cave is especially bright and moist). They are classified as five-colored nails, so they are attached to it.

6. Worm-eaten: Peeling like insect bites (called drilling in the Song Dynasty) is caused by water erosion into holes of different sizes, which is enough to prove the tenderness and moistness of the stone. It is quite interesting if it is outside the ink pool, so scholars value it.

According to other books, there are also so-called ancient spots, cedar patterns, and blood edges, which are all medium and second-class beautiful patterns. There is also a kind of hawksbill spot, which is blue-purple like a turtle shell and has deep purple spots. It is found in the stones of the late Song Dynasty and early Ming Dynasty. The Japanese value it most and call it the Jishui Cliff, which is also rare.

(B) Real Stone Flaws

There are several stone flaws that are really annoying. 1. Iron Thread: It can be broken easily when chiseling it at the skin gap. 2. Water Thread: Like a hard crack. Also known as warning lines. 3. Pig Bristle Eyes: Like the pores of plucked pig bristles, the stone texture does not condense. 4. Oil-Slick Light: Also written as dragonfly light, like oil on the surface of water, it is firm, slippery, and does not accept ink. This is the biggest disease of the old pit. 5. Sand Nail: As big as a finger, it is stubborn and hard like a nail, which is different from the five-colored nail.

Short Story

The Sorrow of the Old Yellow Ox (Continued) 193

— Mingdao

"Silly girl, do you love that old yellow ox so much? What's the benefit of raising it at home until it dies?" "Don't cry, if your father hears you, he will scold you."

Her mother wiped away her tears for her and comforted her, but she would never forget this in her weak heart.

One night passed.

In the morning when the red sun was just rising, A-Shuisheng and Yinbao's mother were about to eat breakfast, but they couldn't find Yinbao. The two of them searched everywhere, and when they walked to the cowshed, they saw Yinbao squatting in front of the old yellow ox, staring at it with a flaw. The old yellow ox was lying on the ground, panting in its mouth, its eyes wide open, and it was also looking at Yinbao.

A-Shuisheng shouted strangely, "Yinbao, why don't you go to eat breakfast? You hid here early in the morning to see the sick ox. Today, it is going to leave us!"

Yinbao squatted on the ground and said to A-Shuisheng, "Dad, is the old yellow ox going to leave us today? But is it sold? It has been with us for many years, and I really can't bear it. It is already sick, and if it is sold to others to be slaughtered, wouldn't it be a sin? Dad, please spare it! Let it live in our house again."

These words, Yinbao seemed to say very pitifully, but unexpectedly touched his father's anger, pulled up his face, and shouted in a refined and violent voice, "What do you kids know! This is an adult's business, and it has nothing to do with you kids. Do you know that your dad has no money to use? In this year, people are also sold, let alone an ox; not to mention an old yellow ox that is sick and about to die and has no strength to cultivate the field! Go to the house quickly, don't nag."

Father's majesty? Yinbao has always known it. He cried with a sad face and dared not say anything more. His mother hugged him and walked towards the house, fearing that A-Shuisheng's old fist would be waved out and Yinbao would be beaten severely.

Before lunch, A-Shuisheng's aunt suddenly came to see the couple from a nearby village. After meeting, she told them the story in detail. It turned out that A-Shuisheng's aunt's husband, A-Kui, had been sick in bed for several days, and his illness was very serious, which made her unable to think of anything, so she had to run here to discuss it.

A-Shuisheng sat impatiently listening to his aunt talk, he just scratched his head, expressing a helpless look.

His aunt was very disappointed and almost cried. So, Yinbao's mother couldn't help but say, "A-Shuisheng, lend five dollars to your aunt. She will have a meeting fee to pay in March next year. I know this is the first meeting of the Zhao family."

So A-Shuisheng nodded and agreed.

The couple invited their aunt to have lunch here, and the customer who bought the ox came. A-Shuisheng first led him to the cowshed to see it, and then came back and sat down. The price had already been negotiated. The customer was a Shandong native, and he took out the snow-white silver dollars very happily and gave them all to A-Shuisheng. A-Shuisheng took it and let the Shandong native lead the sick old yellow ox away.

When the old yellow ox was led out of the cowshed, strangely enough, although it was a beast, it seemed to have spirituality. Knowing that its last day had come, it wailed and resisted, unwilling to leave its owner, its old home, 丨丨丨 the dilapidated cowshed. Yinbao was watching blankly from the side, although he dared not sound in his mouth, how sad he was in his heart! A bag of tears was already full in his small eyes.

In the end, the poor sick old yellow ox followed the Shandong native and left its owner, its old home, its little friend 丨丨 Yinbao. Alas! The slaughterhouse is the place where its lifelong hard work will end! A-Shuisheng's aunt also borrowed five silver dollars and hurried home to save her husband. When she was walking on the road, she thought to herself, when the ox is old and sick, it can still be sold for some money to use, but what about people? Is it possible that people are not as good as oxen?

A-Shuisheng and his wife got the money from selling the ox and discussed how to allocate their uses. Fortunately, they already had the capital to buy a new ox next year. Their plan can temporarily be worry-free.

Yinbao hid in the corner of the room and secretly shed tears, and it can be said that only he understood the sorrow of the old yellow ox.

Pseudo-Organization Participates in the Far Eastern Games

Our Country Consistently Refuses 194

National Sports Association Issues Important Statement

▲ The Sports Association Yesterday Telegraphically Replied to Overseas Chinese in the Philippines

▲ Shen Siliang Denies Allowing Individuals to Participate

The Chinese National Sports Promotion Association, in order to express that our country has always firmly refused the participation of pseudo-organizations in the Far Eastern Games, yesterday specially issued the following announcement:

Recently, news reports have repeatedly seen the matter of Manchuria participating in the Far Eastern Games. There are many discussions, and there is no consensus. All of them are the creation of a certain party to confuse the public. The National Sports Promotion Association has already resolutely refused and has not shown any signs of retreat. The so-called tripartite meeting held in Shanghai is also of the nature of an executive meeting. The Association had specially telegraphed the Philippine Association in advance that the issue of Manchuria's participation should not be raised for discussion when the Association was held in Shanghai.

▲ The Association Telegraphed a Reply to Overseas Chinese in the Philippines

Yesterday, the Association received a telegram from the New China Daily in Manila, inquiring about Manchuria's request to join the Far Eastern Games. After receiving the telegram, the Association immediately replied as follows: "To the New China Daily in Manila, our country has always refused Manchuria to join the Far Eastern Games and has not shown any signs of retreat. National Sports Association, Yan"

▲ Scope of Round Table Conference Discussions

The reporter from the Shishi News Agency visited Mr. Shen Siliang, the main leader of the Sports Association, yesterday. According to Mr. Shen, this round table conference is a kind of ordinary meeting, discussing the various procedures for the current Far Eastern Games. The meeting discussed the scope of the general championship of the conference, and various important cases where friendly matches should be changed to championship matches. It is held as usual before each session and has no other effect. The outside world has been misunderstood due to false rumors and believes that the round table conference, the content is how and how, all belong to speculation. As for the meeting period, it can only be decided after the Philippine and Japanese representatives arrive in Shanghai.

▲ Denial of Allowing Individuals to Participate

Mr. Shen continued, if the Japanese side raises the issue of pseudo-organizations participating, we will seriously refuse, and even withdraw voluntarily, which we will not hesitate to do. The outside world has said that there is a saying of allowing individuals from the pseudo-country to participate, which is unfounded and unpredictable. It is thought that it is all the smoke screen of the Japanese people's false claims of deception (according to Zhang Jiong, director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education, who gave a speech in Beijing on the 27th, saying that if they come to participate in the Far Eastern Games in the name of the pseudo-country, our country will definitely insist, but if they participate as individuals and there is no pseudo-country name, then they will of course be allowed to join). Our authorities are determined to uphold the principle of not losing power and humiliating the country. As for the telegram from the overseas Chinese in Manila, this Association has replied with an explanation.

▲ All Sectors Generously Agreed to Donate Funds

Mr. Shen continued, this Association is now actively preparing for the various procedures for the Far Eastern Games and pre-selection. We previously raised funds from the Shandong Military and Political Authorities and received generous support from all sectors. The future is very optimistic and we have received more than 10,000 yuan in donations. As for the preparations for the pre-selection, the committee is scheduled to meet on April 10 and has now notified all committee members to come to Shanghai to attend.

Questioning National Track and Field Records 197

▲Men's High Jump: Wu Bixian, 1.82 Meters

▲Women's Javelin: Chen Rongming, 27.75 Meters

▲Women's Long Jump: Qian Hangsu, 4.88 Meters

In the national men's and women's track and field highest records for the year 22 of the Republic of China, announced by the China National Amateur Athletic Federation, the following questions have been discovered: (1) In last year's 17th North China Games, the men's high jump performance of Ji Wu Bixian was 1.82 meters, which is better than the 1.81 meters achieved by Hu Gu Huo in last year's National Games. (2) In last year's 3rd Shanghai City Games, the women's javelin performance of Chen Rongming was 27.75 meters, which is better than Chen's own 26.38 meters in last year's National Games. (3) In last year's 3rd Shanghai City Games, the women's long jump performance of Qian Hangsu was 4.88 meters, which is better than Li Yuanfen's 4.795 meters in last year's National Games. For the above three items, the performances exceeding the announced highest records, is it because they could not be established for other reasons, or were they omitted due to reports or collections from various parties? In addition, there are Liu Changchun's 22 seconds flat in the 200-meter preliminary round of the National Games, Zhao Yunshan's 13.4 seconds in the women's 100-meter preliminary round, and Qian Hangsu's 14.3 seconds in the women's 80-meter hurdles preliminary round. Were these preliminary round performances established, or were they not counted for other reasons? The Athletic Federation should provide explanations to dispel public doubts.

Jiangnan University Basketball Yesterday

Jinling Lost to Datong 198

| 15 to 35 |

▲Today Jinling vs. Guanghua at Guanghua

The Jinling University basketball team played its first game against Datong yesterday afternoon at the Datong basketball court, as part of a makeup game for Jiangnan University basketball. The game was evenly matched and fiercely contested. In the first half, both sides defended tightly, making it difficult to score. The score was 8 to 6, with Datong leading by two points. As the second half began, Datong's players suddenly gained momentum. Ren Jiexing and Chen Zhaoqiu weaved through the defense, unstoppable, and scored repeatedly. Jinling was unable to defend, and the situation deteriorated. In the last five minutes, Datong substituted in their second-string players, and Jinling still showed no improvement. In the end, Datong won a great victory with a score of 35 to 15. The referee was Lu Xiangqian. Today at 3 p.m., Jinling will play Guanghua again at Guanghua. Hong Kong Special Silver Shield Tournament

Welsh Wins Championship 199

Defeats South China Three to Zero

(Hong Kong News) Last Saturday (the 24th), the Special Silver Shield final was held, with South China A and Welsh competing. This game was the championship match, so-called success or failure, all depend on this one move, so Hong Kong and Chinese fans are very excited, crowded and very much, all want to see the South China triumphal song. Unexpectedly, the result of the competition, Nanyang was defeated by zero to three, not only the championship was handed over to Welsh, but also suffered the taste of an egg, at the same time disappointed all Hong Kong fans, this is the South China has made the champion hope of this session of the regular cup into a bubble, now send the special silver medal to others, I don't want to say it. In this game, South China's left-winger Ye Beihua was absent from the battle due to an incident, and Wu Baoqu of Group B supplemented his absence, so the lineup was greatly inferior. The five tigers of the forward line were often inaccurate in passing the ball, as if they had lost control. The lack of power in shooting, the lack of courage in the offensive, and the loss of opportunity were even more superfluous. The entire team, except for Li Tiansheng, performed abnormally, so South China's defeat was justified. On the other hand, the Welsh team, 11 players, had close contact and passed the ball quickly, so their victory over South China was really a level higher, not lucky.
