Film Special

Details of the Rasputin Case (Part 2) 275

— Cang Sang

= MGM Accused of Allusion =

= Former Russian Grand Duchess Seeks Compensation for Losses =

Prince Yussupov decided to personally investigate whether Rasputin's harm was true, so he pretended to submit to him and found out that he was licentious and ambitious to usurp the throne. Rasputin drank wildly all day long, thinking that Prince Yussupov was also under his control, so he told him all his treacherous plans, and even revealed his relationship with the Empress. He boasted that the Empress could not lose him, because he could save the Crown Prince today and kill him tomorrow. He also said that he was determined to be the master of all Russia. He also told Prince Yussupov in person the secret that he had been used by Germany. His planned conspiracy was to have the Tsar abdicate and the Empress act as regent, so that he would be no different from the Emperor of Russia.

Prince Yussupov then secretly discussed this matter with courtiers who were loyal to the country. At that time, the Tsar was personally leading the front line, and the police were unable to do anything. They decided to get rid of this powerful traitor, so Prince Yussupov took action himself. Rasputin once boasted that he knew that someone wanted to assassinate him, but no one could hurt a hair on his head. Prince Yao then obtained poison from a doctor that was enough to poison twenty people, and mixed it into wine and cheese. Rasputin ate all the wine and cheese, but there was no movement at all. Prince Yao panicked, so he took out a pistol and shot. Rasputin fell to the ground after being shot, as if he was dead. Soon he came alive again, so Prince Yao fired another shot and threw him into the river. Afterwards, he was arrested and exiled abroad, and his wife followed him. When he was exiled abroad, he could be said to be penniless. Now that they have watched this film, they cannot help but feel emotional and reminisce about the past.

The story of Princess Natasha and Prince Shigodiev's engagement in the film is their story at that time. The various aspects of Rasputin before and after were filmed vividly. The portrayal of Princess Natasha in the film also having a relationship with Rasputin, and Rasputin going to Princess Natasha's place, the plaintiff's lawyer claimed that it actually contained a hint that the princess was Rasputin's lover.

When the princess appeared in court, she was wearing a primary color coat, and her hat was also black. A net covered her eyes, and a bunch of fresh flowers were inserted in her mink collar, which made her even more beautiful. She said that she lived with her mother. When the defendant's lawyer asked, she said that she was the second niece of the late Empress, and she often went to the palace. When the war broke out, she was in Germany, and later managed to escape back to Russia. She had never met Rasputin, but she often heard people talk about him. After the communist revolution, she accompanied the Empress Dowager from Crimea on a British warship to escape. She watched the film and believed that Princess Natasha was alluding to her, and Shigodiev was alluding to her husband. Prince Yao also said the same, and pointed out that the palace scene, depicting Natasha's plight, actually contained the meaning that after she had an affair with Rasputin, Rasputin told her not to make a sound. The princess finally stated to the court that she was prepared to file the same lawsuit in Austria, Germany, France, Italy, the United States, and other countries. (End)

Film Review

Review of "Confessions of a Girl" 276

— Ling He

ParoleGirl 丨 Cathay 丨

American films almost have a common trend. No matter what, they must be light and fast, so that the entertaining audience can be carefree in the time of one hundred and twenty minutes. Therefore, no matter what the subject matter is, even if it is quite real, it must be made as interesting as possible. As for the story that is empty and similar because of the interest, that is naturally even more needless to say.

This is by no means an accidental phenomenon. There are many audiences in the United States who demand a Happyending, and slapstick comedy can sell well. Why shouldn't the producers try their best to meet their demands?

"Confessions of a Girl" also belongs to this type of film.

Regardless of the playwright's explanation that Shelby's scam was for her father's illness, and regardless of the fact that he could not ignore the morbidity of society, this was only to intersperse a rather interesting story for the poor girl.

Regarding the story itself, although it unfolds a certain part of the social phenomenon, perhaps those who are responsible for maintaining law and order will consider it to be an incitement to theft. Isn't it? It teaches you how to scam, and it teaches you how to cheat in prison. However, this film is being publicly screened, so there is nothing to say, perhaps because it is a boring narrative and is not noticed by people.

Indeed, this is an insignificant film. Ordinary, vulgar, even if you have seen it, you will forget it when you walk out of the theater. Obviously, this is because the content is empty. This proves that a work of art must have substantial content, otherwise it will never be able to move people.

Regarding this film, I really don't think there is anything to say. Regardless of whether it is a clear and smooth narrative of a story, and the so-called expression techniques are still very skilled, but in the technically advanced United States, what is so strange about it?

Meek拉克, who plays Xue Erwei, can be considered to have performed well. Perhaps she is the pillar of Columbia? 拉夫伯勒孟, who plays Smith, is worthless, and he is not even qualified to be called competent.

Review of "Pardners" 277

— Sha Si

Pardners 丨 Da Guangming 丨

On the screen, just like on the stage, good actors with talent can certainly make the content of the script have a higher and more effective expression, and even complete an effect that is beyond the author's imagination; but if the content of the script is too empty, this will bind the genius of good actors, making them unable to have sufficient development opportunities, and as a result, their performance in it will become ordinary, lifeless, and without any creative meaning. Even if there is a top-notch director to direct, at most, he can only make some small effects on many small techniques, as for the main overall effect (including the actors' creation), it still cannot be saved. If the script is not good, the actors and directors are useless.

"Pardners" is a very obvious example. It is just a collection of some accidental and meaningless events. There is no certain center. The author seems to want to describe Sikete 丨 played by Jia Kegu Bo 丨 as the center, but the compilation of the script did not fully grasp the center, and the director's technique did not make efforts to remedy such shortcomings. As a result, the impression that "Pardners" gives people is that there is no certain center and no unified effect.

Also, this film did not first express the family situation of Sikete 丨 that is, his father's difficulties and his loneliness 丨 very concretely. This is really a loss for describing Sikete's experience as the center, because if the author concretely expresses it with sympathy, it can strengthen the effect of Sikete in the development of the whole play. In this way, the expression of the center will be strengthened and made more prominent and powerful. But the author and the director do not do this.

In addition, if the interlude of bullfighting, especially that Du Bai saw his runaway wife and her lover in the bullfighting arena, is really too accidental. This is not of much benefit to the development of the whole play and the expression of the center, but just increases the length of the film. In fact, such empty works can only be completed by using such accidental interludes... This is how most European and American film authors make films at present.

Several important actors in "Pardners" are very competent; it is just a pity that they are limited by the content of the script and the lack of creative talent of the director, and because the techniques are not clever, they do not have brilliant and moving performances; especially Jia Kegu Bo, in this film, his performance talent is even more restricted.

Taihua Film Company to be Established 278

The "Baiou" Film Company, which was previously being planned in this port, has now been renamed "Taihua." The company was founded by playwright Zuo Ming and Bao Zhichao. Last month, Zuo and Bao went to Beijing specifically to raise funds, and moved the preparation office to the capital. Now, with the enthusiastic investment from all walks of life in the capital, more than 30,000 yuan has been raised. It is said that the capital is currently tentatively set at 100,000 yuan. When 50,000 yuan is raised, the film will be officially shot. At present, Zuo and others are in Beijing, collecting funds on the one hand, and carrying out company registration and other procedures on the other hand. It is expected that they will be able to return to Shanghai in about a week.

Tianyi's "Special Express" 279

After compiling "Spring Night Serenade", Yu Dingxun is proceeding with the compilation of the new play "Special Express". This special express is from Shanghai to Nanjing. From this short "special express" moment, it will expose the sorrowful climax of the unemployed masses, the powerless shouts, the opening of the bright future, and the struggle in the dark pit one by one, and indicate them one by one. Now, the whole play has been mostly completed.

Film Special Contribution Guidelines 280

This publication is a film publication that promotes culture and art. External contributions are very welcome. Once published, the remuneration will be generous.

Once the text is published, the copyright is owned by Shen Bao.

The text of this publication is mainly in vernacular Chinese and must use new-style punctuation.

If the submission is a translation, it should be accompanied by the original work. If English is mixed in, it should be omitted if possible.

The length of this publication is limited, and the text should be as concise as possible. Each manuscript should be limited to about 500 words.

Unless otherwise stated in advance and return postage is attached, this publication is not responsible for the preservation or return of text, photos, etc.

If dual submissions and plagiarism are found, remuneration will not be given.

Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper, do not write horizontally, and do not use a pencil.

When submitting a manuscript, each article must be affixed with a seal, otherwise it will be treated as a refusal.

Film Novel

Carolina (6) 281

— Wen Yin

Mrs. Connally's stern voice startled Joanna out of her sweet dreams. Mrs. Connally, calling Will, walked up. She said, "Will, isn't this the time you danced with Fotini? She's looking for you." Will and Joanna stood up immediately. Will and Joanna apologized, glanced at her, and slipped away. Joanna was about to walk away, but Mrs. Connally stopped her, so she stood still. Connally talked to her a lot, and his words were firm, powerful, and cold. After he finished speaking, he said to Joanna, "My dear, you probably understand, don't you?" Joanna said, "I understand, Mrs. Connally." Mrs. Connally said, "Then you should be a knowledgeable woman, and from now on, you can't think about Will anymore." Her voice was extremely kind, because she felt that victory already belonged to her. It was such an easy thing to do! Unexpectedly, Joanna was not easy to get up. She said, "Mrs. Connally, I can't promise you this." Connally's face immediately changed, but she still used a gentle and strong tone, and said to Joanna, "Listen to me, don't meet him again..." After she finished speaking, she said good night and went back in a hurry. Here Joanna still wanted to chase after her and talk to Connally, but suddenly a person walked up from the darkness. It was old Robert. In his old eyes, Joanna was not Joanna, but Barbara, and she was wearing a fashion from decades ago. She whispered to Joanna, "Be careful, don't let Allen see us." Allen was Mrs. Connally's name, but Joanna didn't know. She asked repeatedly, "What's the matter, Mr. Robert?" Robert said, "My darling! My beautiful..." He stretched out his arms to hug her. He said, "Where have you been? I'm always waiting... This is almost a hundred years... We only have a moment together... The army is advancing... What did Allen just say to you?" Robert's attitude was extremely strange. She understood that Allen was Mrs. Connally, but she was very scared. She took a step back and said with horror, "She...she..." Robert said, "Let's not care about her." She is always against us, since the day she saw us kissing." He hugged Joanna, his mouth looking for her mouth. He shouted, "My dearest love...my dearest love!"

Joanna pushed him away with all her might, shouting, "Mr. Robert, don't do this!" She wanted to run away, but Robert stopped her and said, "Don't be afraid, I will come back from the battlefield, I will come back..." He bent down and kissed the edge of her skirt. In his eyes, it was not a cotton dress, but a new dress made of fine silk. He stretched out his hand again to grab her, saying, "Let me kiss you goodbye." Joanna shouted loudly, "Mr. Robert!" Robert stared blankly, as if he was gradually waking up from a dream. He said vaguely, "What did you call me? "Mr. Robert"? This is all wrong... That was many years ago... I will remember it... Tomorrow... I will remember it..." Will ran back in a hurry, shouting to Robert, "Uncle, you scared her to death." Robert chuckled and said, "Scared her to death? Me? You don't know." He walked away staggeringly. He was still talking to himself, "What will Allen do? I'm going to tell her that she's back..." (To be continued)
